2. Event Handler Functions ^8t5te39y

ðŸ‘‰    Code that lives at the top level of the component function

ðŸ‘‰    Participates in describing how the component view looks like

ðŸ‘‰    Executed every time the component renders ^nAK9rZRk

ðŸ‘‰    Executed as a consequence of the event that the handler is listening for
        (change event in this example)

ðŸ‘‰    Code that actually does things: update state, perform an HTTP request, read an input field
        navigate to another page, etc...
 ^CvCz0pVJ

function Question({question}){
        const [newAnswer, setNewAnswer] = useState('')
        const numAnswers = question.answers.length ?? 0;

        const handleNewAsnwer = function(e){
                if (question.closed) return;
                setNewAnswer(e.target.value)        
        }

        const createList = function(){
                return (
                        <ul>
                                {question.answers.map((q) => (
                                        <li>{q}</li>
                                ))}
                        </ul>
                )
        }

        return (
        <div>
                <h3>{question.title}</h3>
                <p>{question.body}</p>
                {question.hasAnswer} ? (
                        createList()
                ) : (
                        <input value={newAnswer} onChange={handleNewAnswer} />
                )
        )
} ^wUP5D2K5
